                        function checkZaloIsOpened(){
            if (jQuery('#ar-zalo-chat-widget>div').height() < 100){ 
                jQuery('#ar-zalo-chat-widget').removeClass('active');
                jQuery('#arcontactus').contactUs('show');
                clearInterval(zaloWidgetInterval);
            }
        }
